def Scope "Looks"
{
    def Material "pxrUsdPreviewSurface1SG"
    {
        token outputs:surface.connect = </Looks/pxrUsdPreviewSurface1SG/MiniChainsawShader.outputs:surface>

        def Shader "MiniChainsawShader"
        {
            uniform token info:id = "UsdPreviewSurface"
            color3f inputs:diffuseColor.connect = </Looks/pxrUsdPreviewSurface1SG/tex_base.outputs:rgb>
            float inputs:metallic = 0
            float inputs:occlusion = 0
            float inputs:roughness = 1
            token outputs:surface
        }

        def Shader "tex_base"
        {
            uniform token info:id = "UsdUVTexture"
            float4 inputs:fallback = (0.5, 0.5, 0.5, 1)
            asset inputs:file = @0/MiniChainsaw_baseColor.jpg@
            float2 inputs:st.connect = </Looks/pxrUsdPreviewSurface1SG/tex_base/TexCoordReader.outputs:result>
            float3 outputs:rgb

            def Shader "TexCoordReader"
            {
                uniform token info:id = "UsdPrimVarReader_float2"
                token inputs:varname = "st"
                float2 outputs:result
            }
        }
    }
